        <div id="readme" class="Box-body readme blob js-code-block-container p-5 p-xl-6 gist-border-0">
    <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-无人驾驶" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#无人驾驶"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>无人驾驶</h1>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-1数据采集以及数据预处理" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#1数据采集以及数据预处理"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>1.数据采集以及数据预处理</h2>
<p dir="auto">1.arduino烧录小车网页控制和摄像头代码。</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220826194412500.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220826194412500.png" alt="image-20220826194412500" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">2.网页遥控小车按地图行驶，并定时拍照。</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220826194304322.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220826194304322.png" alt="image-20220826194304322" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">3.收集拍摄的照片，初步筛选数据，将重复度高，成像不清等不符合训练要求的图像删除。</p>
<p dir="auto">4.登录Easydata，新建图像分割-语义分割数据集，将未打标签的照片上传。</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822134929390.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822134929390.png" alt="image-20220822134929390" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">5.创建完成后，进入Easydata的“查看与标签”功能，标记出图像中的background和grass，这样剩下的部分即为road。<strong>需要注意的是建立标签的顺序，这里演示的为先新建background标签，再建grass标签，这一点在后面生成masks图像的时候会稍有影响。</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822135135007.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822135135007.png" alt="image-20220822135135007" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822135609714.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822135609714.png" alt="image-20220822135609714" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">6.标注完成后，点击开始导出后，待导出完成即可下载到本地。</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822140330817.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822140330817.png" alt="image-20220822140330817" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822140422371.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822140422371.png" alt="image-20220822140422371" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">导出的压缩包解压后如图所示，有两个文件夹和一个txt文件，其中“JPEGAImages”文件夹内部是原图数据，"SegmentationClass"文件夹里面是标签数据图片，txt文件里面是</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220822140542615.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220822140542615.png" alt="image-20220822140542615" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-2软件安装与环境配置" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#2软件安装与环境配置"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>2.软件安装与环境配置</h2>
<p dir="auto">1.安装VScode和anaconda3，打开电脑command，输入“conda”+回车，检查anaconda是否已经添加到环境中，若报错没有该命令，则需要将anaconda3对应目录下的的 ..\ANACONDA\condabin 路径和 ..\ANACONDA\Library\bin 路径添加到系统环境中，可以在系统设置中搜索“环境”。</p>
<p dir="auto">2.在command中输入：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="conda create -n name python=3.7  "><pre class="notranslate"><code>conda create -n name python=3.7  
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">新建虚拟环境，其中name是自行设置的环境名，可以指定python版本，这里以python3.7为例                 <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822101828295.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822101828295.png" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">3.command输入：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="conda activate name    #进入虚拟环境"><pre class="notranslate"><code>conda activate name    #进入虚拟环境
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822102607980.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822102607980.png" alt="image-20220822102607980" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">4.在虚拟环境中安装依赖的python库：在项目文件中有一个packages.txt文件，里面包含了本项目所需要的全部python库的名称，你可以下载下来本文件后，command cd 至指定目录，运行：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="pip install -r packages.txt -i https://pypi.tuna.tsinghua.edu.cn/simple  #清华源"><pre class="notranslate"><code>pip install -r packages.txt -i https://pypi.tuna.tsinghua.edu.cn/simple  #清华源
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822102718800.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822102718800.png" alt="image-20220822102718800" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">即可一键配置好本项目所用python环境。</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822105323007.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822105323007.png" alt="image-20220822105323007" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822105420411.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822105420411.png" alt="image-20220822105420411" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">5.VScode安装python插件：点击左侧插件栏，搜索python，一般第一个即为微软认证的python插件，点击下载安装即可。</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822143529033.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822143529033.png" alt="image-20220822143529033" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">6.获取配置好的虚拟环境的python路径：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="where python"><pre class="notranslate"><code>where python
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822142132912.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822142132912.png" alt="image-20220822142132912" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">将获取的第一个python路径复制下来，打开VScode的设置</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822141859765.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822141859765.png" alt="image-20220822141859765" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822141937088.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822141937088.png" alt="image-20220822141937088" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">在设置搜索栏搜索“python interpreter”，将刚刚复制的路径粘贴在“工作区”的Default Interpreter Path下，这项指仅给当前项目配置该环境，当然也可以把用户的Default Interpreter Path也粘贴上该路径，设置您默认使用的环境，依据您自己的需要而定。</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822142551695.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220822142551695.png" alt="image-20220822142551695" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-3mask" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#3mask"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>3.Mask</h2>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#PATH：\car_project\mask_get"><pre class="notranslate"><code>#PATH：\car_project\mask_get
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">1.查看easydata导出的数据：</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220822162451878.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220822162451878.png" alt="image-20220822162451878" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>

<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="\car_project\mask_get                                #mask_get项目总路径

<p dir="auto">2.用VScode打开项目目录，目录配置好了之后，直接运行就可以在mask目录下生成mask图片数据。</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220822173350415.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220822173350415.png" alt="image-20220822173350415" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">需要注意的是，如果您第一个新建的标签为grass，图中红框标注代码应改为：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="grass_layer = rgb_mask[:, :, 1] / 128         
background_layer = rgb_mask[:, :, 2] / 128 "><pre><span class="pl-s1">grass_layer</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">rgb_mask</span>[:, :, <span class="pl-c1">1</span>] <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">128</span>         
<span class="pl-s1">background_layer</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">rgb_mask</span>[:, :, <span class="pl-c1">2</span>] <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">128</span> </pre></div>
<p dir="auto">3.生成mask图片数据后，您可以用temp.py简单检验一下,随机选一个mask，将其路径填入函数中：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#\car_project\mask_get\temp.py

<p dir="auto">运行，再打开对应的照片比对一下：</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220822175048296.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220822175048296.png" alt="image-20220822175048296" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">红框所圈起来的数字：0对应road；1对应grass；2对应background，确保验证无误。</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-4unet神经网络" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#4unet神经网络"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>4.Unet神经网络</h2>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#PATH：\car_project\unet_torch"><pre class="notranslate"><code>#PATH：\car_project\unet_torch
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Unet 发表于 2015 年，属于 FCN 的一种变体。Unet 的初衷是为了解决生物医学图像方面的问题，由于效果确实很好后来也被广泛的应用在语义分割的各个方向，比如卫星图像分割，工业瑕疵检测等。</p>
<p dir="auto">Unet 跟 FCN 都是 Encoder-Decoder 结构，具体表现为，先对图像进行下采样（池化、卷积等），提取特征，再进行上采样（转置卷积、上池化等），将特征分配给每一个像素点。Encoder 负责特征提取，Decoder负责将特征图恢复原始分辨率。</p>
<p dir="auto">1.我们可以通过训练的主程序了解一下，训练无人驾驶模型的代码的结构（如注释所示）</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#PATH：\car_project\unet_torch\train.py
def train_net(net,
              device,                        #参数对应为：
              epochs: int = 5,               #迭代次数
              batch_size: int = 1,           #批量大小
              learning_rate: float = 1e-5,   #学习率 
              val_percent: float = 0.1,      #验证集比例
              save_checkpoint: bool = True,  #储存checkpoint二进制文件
              img_scale: float = 0.5,        #缩放大小
              amp: bool = False):
    # 1.创建数据集 装载图片与mask标签
    try:
        dataset = CarvanaDataset(dir_img, dir_mask, img_scale)
    except (AssertionError, RuntimeError):
        dataset = BasicDataset(dir_img, dir_mask, img_scale)

    # 2.将数据集分为验证集与训练集 
    n_val = int(len(dataset) * val_percent)  
    n_train = len(dataset) - n_val
    train_set, val_set = random_split(dataset, [n_train, n_val], generator=torch.Generator().manual_seed(0))     #随机选出一定比例的验证集和训练集

    # 3.创建数据装载器 
    loader_args = dict(batch_size=batch_size, num_workers=1, pin_memory=False)  #num_workers:多线程读取数据 
    train_loader = DataLoader(train_set, shuffle=True,**loader_args)
    val_loader = DataLoader(val_set, shuffle=False, drop_last=True, **loader_args)

    # 4. 设置优化算法，学习率调度器，损失函数r，以及AMP（自动混合精度）
    optimizer = optim.RMSprop(net.parameters(), lr=learning_rate, weight_decay=1e-8, momentum=0.9) #优化算法
    scheduler = optim.lr_scheduler.ReduceLROnPlateau(optimizer, 'max', patience=2) #学习率调度器来最大化Dice度   
    grad_scaler = torch.cuda.amp.GradScaler(enabled=amp)                                                         criterion = nn.CrossEntropyLoss()                  #损失函数
    global_step = 0
    # 5.开始训练
    for epoch in range(1, epochs+1):  #迭代设置的次数
        net.train()                 
        epoch_loss = 0                #记录loss值
        with tqdm(total=n_train, desc=f'Epoch {epoch}/{epochs}', unit='img') as pbar:
            for batch in train_loader:      #对每一批次数据的图像，mask标签
                images = batch['image']     #取出图像
                true_masks = batch['mask']  #取出标签

                assert images.shape[1] == net.n_channels, \
                    f'Network has been defined with {net.n_channels} input channels, ' \
                    f'but loaded images have {images.shape[1]} channels. Please check that ' \
                    'the images are loaded correctly.'

                images = images.to(device=device, dtype=torch.float32)      #指定训练用到gpu装置
                true_masks = true_masks.to(device=device, dtype=torch.long)

                with torch.cuda.amp.autocast(enabled=amp):
                    masks_pred = net(images)  
                    loss = criterion(masks_pred, true_masks) \               #损失计算
                           + dice_loss(F.softmax(masks_pred, dim=1).float(),
                                       F.one_hot(true_masks, net.n_classes).permute(0, 3, 1, 2).float(),
                                       multiclass=True)

                optimizer.zero_grad(set_to_none=True)
                grad_scaler.scale(loss).backward()  #根据loss反向传播，
                grad_scaler.step(optimizer)
                grad_scaler.update()

                pbar.update(images.shape[0])   #编辑一些输出的信息，方便用户获取训练的信息
                global_step += 1          
                epoch_loss += loss.item() 
               
                pbar.set_postfix(**{'loss (batch)': loss.item()})

                # Evaluation round
                division_step = (n_train // (10 * batch_size))
                if division_step &gt; 0:
                    if global_step % division_step == 0:
                        val_score = evaluate(net, val_loader, device)
                        scheduler.step(val_score)
        if save_checkpoint:
            Path(dir_checkpoint).mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
            torch.save(net.state_dict(), str(dir_checkpoint / 'checkpoint_epoch{}.pth'.format(epoch)))
            logging.info(f'Checkpoint {epoch} saved!')
            
            def get_args():   #读取用户设置的参数
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description='Train the UNet on images and target masks')
    parser.add_argument('--epochs', '-e', metavar='E', type=int, default=5, help='Number of epochs')#迭代次数
    parser.add_argument('--batch-size', '-b', dest='batch_size', metavar='B', type=int, default=1, help='Batch size')                                                                                  #批量大小
    parser.add_argument('--learning-rate', '-l', metavar='LR', type=float, default=1e-5,
                        help='Learning rate', dest='lr')                                            #学习率
    parser.add_argument('--load', '-f', type=str, default=False, help='Load model from a .pth file')
    parser.add_argument('--scale', '-s', type=float, default=0.5, 
                        help='Downscaling factor of the images')                               #放缩图像的大小
    
    parser.add_argument('--validation', '-v', dest='val', type=float, default=10.0,
                        help='Percent of the data that is used as validation (0-100)')            #验证集比例
    parser.add_argument('--amp', action='store_true', default=False, help='Use mixed precision') 
    parser.add_argument('--bilinear', action='store_true', default=False, help='Use bilinear upsampling')
    parser.add_argument('--classes', '-c', type=int, default=2, help='Number of classes')          #类别数

    return parser.parse_args()


if __name__ == '__main__':

       dir_img = Path('photos\photos_original')      #原图像数据集目录
       dir_mask = Path('photos\masks')               #mask标签图像数据目录
       dir_checkpoint = Path('checkpoint_new')       #checkpoint训练得到的参数保存目录
           
       args = get_args()

       logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(levelname)s: %(message)s')
       device = torch.device('cuda' if torch.cuda.is_available() else 'cpu')
        logging.info(f'Using device {device}')

    
    #n_channel 彩色图片rgb三个通道 
    # n_classes 指所有像素点被分为的类别数
    net = UNet(n_channels=3, n_classes=args.classes, bilinear=args.bilinear)
    
    logging.info(f'Network:\n'
                 f'\t{net.n_channels} input channels\n'
                 f'\t{net.n_classes} output channels (classes)\n'
                 f'\t{&quot;Bilinear&quot; if net.bilinear else &quot;Transposed conv&quot;} upscaling')

    if args.load:
        net.load_state_dict(torch.load(args.load, map_location=device))
        logging.info(f'Model loaded from {args.load}')

    net.to(device=device)
    # print(summary(net, (3, 800, 600), 4, &quot;cuda&quot;))
    try:
        train_net(net=net,
                  epochs=args.epochs,
                  batch_size=args.batch_size,
                  learning_rate=args.lr,
                  device=device,
                  img_scale=args.scale,
                  val_percent=args.val / 100,
                  amp=args.amp)
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        torch.save(net.state_dict(), 'INTERRUPTED.pth')
        logging.info('Saved interrupt')
        raise
"><pre><span class="pl-c">#PATH：\car_project\unet_torch\train.py</span>
<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">train_net</span>(<span class="pl-s1">net</span>,
              <span class="pl-s1">device</span>,                        <span class="pl-c">#参数对应为：</span>
              <span class="pl-s1">epochs</span>: <span class="pl-s1">int</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span>,               <span class="pl-c">#迭代次数</span>
              <span class="pl-s1">batch_size</span>: <span class="pl-s1">int</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>,           <span class="pl-c">#批量大小</span>
              <span class="pl-s1">learning_rate</span>: <span class="pl-s1">float</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1e-5</span>,   <span class="pl-c">#学习率 </span>

              <span class="pl-s1">img_scale</span>: <span class="pl-s1">float</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.5</span>,        <span class="pl-c">#缩放大小</span>

    <span class="pl-k">except</span> (<span class="pl-v">AssertionError</span>, <span class="pl-v">RuntimeError</span>):
        <span class="pl-s1">dataset</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">BasicDataset</span>(<span class="pl-s1">dir_img</span>, <span class="pl-s1">dir_mask</span>, <span class="pl-s1">img_scale</span>)

    <span class="pl-c"># 2.将数据集分为验证集与训练集 </span>

    <span class="pl-s1">n_train</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">len</span>(<span class="pl-s1">dataset</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">n_val</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">train_set</span>, <span class="pl-s1">val_set</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">random_split</span>(<span class="pl-s1">dataset</span>, [<span class="pl-s1">n_train</span>, <span class="pl-s1">n_val</span>], <span class="pl-s1">generator</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">torch</span>.<span class="pl-v">Generator</span>().<span class="pl-en">manual_seed</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>))     <span class="pl-c">#随机选出一定比例的验证集和训练集</span>

    <span class="pl-s1">loader_args</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">dict</span>(<span class="pl-s1">batch_size</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">batch_size</span>, <span class="pl-s1">num_workers</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span>, <span class="pl-s1">pin_memory</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">False</span>)  <span class="pl-c">#num_workers:多线程读取数据 </span>
    <span class="pl-s1">train_loader</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">DataLoader</span>(<span class="pl-s1">train_set</span>, <span class="pl-s1">shuffle</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">True</span>,<span class="pl-c1">**</span><span class="pl-s1">loader_args</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">val_loader</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">DataLoader</span>(<span class="pl-s1">val_set</span>, <span class="pl-s1">shuffle</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">False</span>, <span class="pl-s1">drop_last</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">True</span>, <span class="pl-c1">**</span><span class="pl-s1">loader_args</span>)

    <span class="pl-c"># 4. 设置优化算法，学习率调度器，损失函数r，以及AMP（自动混合精度）</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">optimizer</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">optim</span>.<span class="pl-v">RMSprop</span>(<span class="pl-s1">net</span>.<span class="pl-en">parameters</span>(), <span class="pl-s1">lr</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">learning_rate</span>, <span class="pl-s1">weight_decay</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">1e-8</span>, <span class="pl-s1">momentum</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">0.9</span>) <span class="pl-c">#优化算法</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">scheduler</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">optim</span>.<span class="pl-s1">lr_scheduler</span>.<span class="pl-v">ReduceLROnPlateau</span>(<span class="pl-s1">optimizer</span>, <span class="pl-s">'max'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">patience</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">2</span>) <span class="pl-c">#学习率调度器来最大化Dice度   </span>
    <span class="pl-s1">grad_scaler</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">torch</span>.<span class="pl-s1">cuda</span>.<span class="pl-s1">amp</span>.<span class="pl-v">GradScaler</span>(<span class="pl-s1">enabled</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">amp</span>)                                                         <span class="pl-s1">criterion</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">nn</span>.<span class="pl-v">CrossEntropyLoss</span>()                  <span class="pl-c">#损失函数</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">global_step</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>
    <span class="pl-c"># 5.开始训练</span>
    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">epoch</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">range</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>, <span class="pl-s1">epochs</span><span class="pl-c1">+</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span>):  <span class="pl-c">#迭代设置的次数</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">net</span>.<span class="pl-en">train</span>()                 
        <span class="pl-s1">epoch_loss</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>                <span class="pl-c">#记录loss值</span>
        <span class="pl-k">with</span> <span class="pl-en">tqdm</span>(<span class="pl-s1">total</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">n_train</span>, <span class="pl-s1">desc</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">f'Epoch <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">epoch</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>/<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">epochs</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">unit</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'img'</span>) <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s1">pbar</span>:
            <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">batch</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">train_loader</span>:      <span class="pl-c">#对每一批次数据的图像，mask标签</span>
                <span class="pl-s1">images</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">batch</span>[<span class="pl-s">'image'</span>]     <span class="pl-c">#取出图像</span>
                <span class="pl-s1">true_masks</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">batch</span>[<span class="pl-s">'mask'</span>]  <span class="pl-c">#取出标签</span>

                <span class="pl-k">assert</span> <span class="pl-s1">images</span>.<span class="pl-s1">shape</span>[<span class="pl-c1">1</span>] <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s1">net</span>.<span class="pl-s1">n_channels</span>, \
                    <span class="pl-s">f'Network has been defined with <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">net</span>.<span class="pl-s1">n_channels</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span> input channels, '</span> \
                    <span class="pl-s">f'but loaded images have <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">images</span>.<span class="pl-s1">shape</span>[<span class="pl-c1">1</span>]<span class="pl-kos">}</span></span> channels. Please check that '</span> \
                    <span class="pl-s">'the images are loaded correctly.'</span>

                <span class="pl-s1">images</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">images</span>.<span class="pl-en">to</span>(<span class="pl-s1">device</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">device</span>, <span class="pl-s1">dtype</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">torch</span>.<span class="pl-s1">float32</span>)      <span class="pl-c">#指定训练用到gpu装置</span>
                <span class="pl-s1">true_masks</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">true_masks</span>.<span class="pl-en">to</span>(<span class="pl-s1">device</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">device</span>, <span class="pl-s1">dtype</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">torch</span>.<span class="pl-s1">long</span>)

                <span class="pl-k">with</span> <span class="pl-s1">torch</span>.<span class="pl-s1">cuda</span>.<span class="pl-s1">amp</span>.<span class="pl-en">autocast</span>(<span class="pl-s1">enabled</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">amp</span>):
                    <span class="pl-s1">masks_pred</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">net</span>(<span class="pl-s1">images</span>)  
                    <span class="pl-s1">loss</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">criterion</span>(<span class="pl-s1">masks_pred</span>, <span class="pl-s1">true_masks</span>) \               <span class="pl-c">#损失计算</span>
                           <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-en">dice_loss</span>(<span class="pl-v">F</span>.<span class="pl-en">softmax</span>(<span class="pl-s1">masks_pred</span>, <span class="pl-s1">dim</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span>).<span class="pl-en">float</span>(),
                                       <span class="pl-v">F</span>.<span class="pl-en">one_hot</span>(<span class="pl-s1">true_masks</span>, <span class="pl-s1">net</span>.<span class="pl-s1">n_classes</span>).<span class="pl-en">permute</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">3</span>, <span class="pl-c1">1</span>, <span class="pl-c1">2</span>).<span class="pl-en">float</span>(),
                                       <span class="pl-s1">multiclass</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">True</span>)

                <span class="pl-s1">optimizer</span>.<span class="pl-en">zero_grad</span>(<span class="pl-s1">set_to_none</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">True</span>)
                <span class="pl-s1">grad_scaler</span>.<span class="pl-en">scale</span>(<span class="pl-s1">loss</span>).<span class="pl-en">backward</span>()  <span class="pl-c">#根据loss反向传播，</span>
                <span class="pl-s1">grad_scaler</span>.<span class="pl-en">step</span>(<span class="pl-s1">optimizer</span>)
                <span class="pl-s1">grad_scaler</span>.<span class="pl-en">update</span>()

                <span class="pl-s1">pbar</span>.<span class="pl-en">update</span>(<span class="pl-s1">images</span>.<span class="pl-s1">shape</span>[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>])   <span class="pl-c">#编辑一些输出的信息，方便用户获取训练的信息</span>
                <span class="pl-s1">global_step</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>          
                <span class="pl-s1">epoch_loss</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s1">loss</span>.<span class="pl-en">item</span>() 
               
                <span class="pl-s1">pbar</span>.<span class="pl-en">set_postfix</span>(<span class="pl-c1">**</span>{<span class="pl-s">'loss (batch)'</span>: <span class="pl-s1">loss</span>.<span class="pl-en">item</span>()})

                <span class="pl-c"># Evaluation round</span>
                <span class="pl-s1">division_step</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> (<span class="pl-s1">n_train</span> <span class="pl-c1">//</span> (<span class="pl-c1">10</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">batch_size</span>))
                <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">division_step</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>:
                    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">global_step</span> <span class="pl-c1">%</span> <span class="pl-s1">division_step</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>:
                        <span class="pl-s1">val_score</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">evaluate</span>(<span class="pl-s1">net</span>, <span class="pl-s1">val_loader</span>, <span class="pl-s1">device</span>)
                        <span class="pl-s1">scheduler</span>.<span class="pl-en">step</span>(<span class="pl-s1">val_score</span>)
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">save_checkpoint</span>:
            <span class="pl-v">Path</span>(<span class="pl-s1">dir_checkpoint</span>).<span class="pl-en">mkdir</span>(<span class="pl-s1">parents</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">True</span>, <span class="pl-s1">exist_ok</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">True</span>)
            <span class="pl-s1">torch</span>.<span class="pl-en">save</span>(<span class="pl-s1">net</span>.<span class="pl-en">state_dict</span>(), <span class="pl-en">str</span>(<span class="pl-s1">dir_checkpoint</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s">'checkpoint_epoch{}.pth'</span>.<span class="pl-en">format</span>(<span class="pl-s1">epoch</span>)))
            <span class="pl-s1">logging</span>.<span class="pl-en">info</span>(<span class="pl-s">f'Checkpoint <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">epoch</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span> saved!'</span>)
            
            <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">get_args</span>():   <span class="pl-c">#读取用户设置的参数</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">parser</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">argparse</span>.<span class="pl-v">ArgumentParser</span>(<span class="pl-s1">description</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'Train the UNet on images and target masks'</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">parser</span>.<span class="pl-en">add_argument</span>(<span class="pl-s">'--epochs'</span>, <span class="pl-s">'-e'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">metavar</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'E'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">type</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">int</span>, <span class="pl-s1">default</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">5</span>, <span class="pl-s1">help</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'Number of epochs'</span>)<span class="pl-c">#迭代次数</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">parser</span>.<span class="pl-en">add_argument</span>(<span class="pl-s">'--batch-size'</span>, <span class="pl-s">'-b'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">dest</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'batch_size'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">metavar</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'B'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">type</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">int</span>, <span class="pl-s1">default</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span>, <span class="pl-s1">help</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'Batch size'</span>)                                                                                  <span class="pl-c">#批量大小</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">parser</span>.<span class="pl-en">add_argument</span>(<span class="pl-s">'--learning-rate'</span>, <span class="pl-s">'-l'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">metavar</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'LR'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">type</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">float</span>, <span class="pl-s1">default</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">1e-5</span>,
                        <span class="pl-s1">help</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'Learning rate'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">dest</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'lr'</span>)                                            <span class="pl-c">#学习率</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">parser</span>.<span class="pl-en">add_argument</span>(<span class="pl-s">'--load'</span>, <span class="pl-s">'-f'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">type</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">str</span>, <span class="pl-s1">default</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">False</span>, <span class="pl-s1">help</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'Load model from a .pth file'</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">parser</span>.<span class="pl-en">add_argument</span>(<span class="pl-s">'--scale'</span>, <span class="pl-s">'-s'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">type</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">float</span>, <span class="pl-s1">default</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">0.5</span>, 
                        <span class="pl-s1">help</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'Downscaling factor of the images'</span>)                               <span class="pl-c">#放缩图像的大小</span>
    
    <span class="pl-s1">parser</span>.<span class="pl-en">add_argument</span>(<span class="pl-s">'--validation'</span>, <span class="pl-s">'-v'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">dest</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'val'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">type</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">float</span>, <span class="pl-s1">default</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">10.0</span>,
                        <span class="pl-s1">help</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'Percent of the data that is used as validation (0-100)'</span>)            <span class="pl-c">#验证集比例</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">parser</span>.<span class="pl-en">add_argument</span>(<span class="pl-s">'--amp'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">action</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'store_true'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">default</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">False</span>, <span class="pl-s1">help</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'Use mixed precision'</span>) 
    <span class="pl-s1">parser</span>.<span class="pl-en">add_argument</span>(<span class="pl-s">'--bilinear'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">action</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'store_true'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">default</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">False</span>, <span class="pl-s1">help</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'Use bilinear upsampling'</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">parser</span>.<span class="pl-en">add_argument</span>(<span class="pl-s">'--classes'</span>, <span class="pl-s">'-c'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">type</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">int</span>, <span class="pl-s1">default</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">2</span>, <span class="pl-s1">help</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'Number of classes'</span>)          <span class="pl-c">#类别数</span>

    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">parser</span>.<span class="pl-en">parse_args</span>()


<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">__name__</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">'__main__'</span>:

       <span class="pl-s1">dir_img</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Path</span>(<span class="pl-s">'photos\photos_original'</span>)      <span class="pl-c">#原图像数据集目录</span>
       <span class="pl-s1">dir_mask</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Path</span>(<span class="pl-s">'photos\masks'</span>)               <span class="pl-c">#mask标签图像数据目录</span>
       <span class="pl-s1">dir_checkpoint</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Path</span>(<span class="pl-s">'checkpoint_new'</span>)       <span class="pl-c">#checkpoint训练得到的参数保存目录</span>
           
       <span class="pl-s1">args</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">get_args</span>()

       <span class="pl-s1">logging</span>.<span class="pl-en">basicConfig</span>(<span class="pl-s1">level</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">logging</span>.<span class="pl-v">INFO</span>, <span class="pl-s1">format</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'%(levelname)s: %(message)s'</span>)
       <span class="pl-s1">device</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">torch</span>.<span class="pl-en">device</span>(<span class="pl-s">'cuda'</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">torch</span>.<span class="pl-s1">cuda</span>.<span class="pl-en">is_available</span>() <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-s">'cpu'</span>)
        <span class="pl-s1">logging</span>.<span class="pl-en">info</span>(<span class="pl-s">f'Using device <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">device</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>'</span>)

    
    <span class="pl-c">#n_channel 彩色图片rgb三个通道 </span>
    <span class="pl-c"># n_classes 指所有像素点被分为的类别数</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">net</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">UNet</span>(<span class="pl-s1">n_channels</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">3</span>, <span class="pl-s1">n_classes</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">args</span>.<span class="pl-s1">classes</span>, <span class="pl-s1">bilinear</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">args</span>.<span class="pl-s1">bilinear</span>)
    
    <span class="pl-s1">logging</span>.<span class="pl-en">info</span>(<span class="pl-s">f'Network:<span class="pl-cce">\n</span>'</span>
                 <span class="pl-s">f'<span class="pl-cce">\t</span><span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">net</span>.<span class="pl-s1">n_channels</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span> input channels<span class="pl-cce">\n</span>'</span>
                 <span class="pl-s">f'<span class="pl-cce">\t</span><span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">net</span>.<span class="pl-s1">n_classes</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span> output channels (classes)<span class="pl-cce">\n</span>'</span>
                 <span class="pl-s">f'<span class="pl-cce">\t</span><span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s">"Bilinear"</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">net</span>.<span class="pl-s1">bilinear</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-s">"Transposed conv"</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span> upscaling'</span>)

    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">args</span>.<span class="pl-s1">load</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">net</span>.<span class="pl-en">load_state_dict</span>(<span class="pl-s1">torch</span>.<span class="pl-en">load</span>(<span class="pl-s1">args</span>.<span class="pl-s1">load</span>, <span class="pl-s1">map_location</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">device</span>))
        <span class="pl-s1">logging</span>.<span class="pl-en">info</span>(<span class="pl-s">f'Model loaded from <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">args</span>.<span class="pl-s1">load</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>'</span>)

    <span class="pl-s1">net</span>.<span class="pl-en">to</span>(<span class="pl-s1">device</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">device</span>)
    <span class="pl-c"># print(summary(net, (3, 800, 600), 4, "cuda"))</span>
    <span class="pl-k">try</span>:
        <span class="pl-en">train_net</span>(<span class="pl-s1">net</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">net</span>,
                  <span class="pl-s1">epochs</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">args</span>.<span class="pl-s1">epochs</span>,
                  <span class="pl-s1">batch_size</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">args</span>.<span class="pl-s1">batch_size</span>,
                  <span class="pl-s1">learning_rate</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">args</span>.<span class="pl-s1">lr</span>,
                  <span class="pl-s1">device</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">device</span>,
                  <span class="pl-s1">img_scale</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">args</span>.<span class="pl-s1">scale</span>,
                  <span class="pl-s1">val_percent</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">args</span>.<span class="pl-s1">val</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">100</span>,
                  <span class="pl-s1">amp</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">args</span>.<span class="pl-s1">amp</span>)
    <span class="pl-k">except</span> <span class="pl-v">KeyboardInterrupt</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">torch</span>.<span class="pl-en">save</span>(<span class="pl-s1">net</span>.<span class="pl-en">state_dict</span>(), <span class="pl-s">'INTERRUPTED.pth'</span>)
        <span class="pl-s1">logging</span>.<span class="pl-en">info</span>(<span class="pl-s">'Saved interrupt'</span>)
        <span class="pl-k">raise</span></pre></div>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="模型结构文件路径：\car_project\unet_torch\unet
模型结构快定义文件路径：\car_project\unet_torch\unet
数据装载文件路径：\car_project\unet_torch\utils"><pre class="notranslate"><code>模型结构文件路径：\car_project\unet_torch\unet
模型结构快定义文件路径：\car_project\unet_torch\unet
数据装载文件路径：\car_project\unet_torch\utils
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">2.在本地电脑试运行一下训练模型的代码：打开command终端，进入虚拟环境，cd至train.py目录下，输入命令(例)：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="python train.py -l 0.0002 -s 0.5 -e 2 -c 3 -b 4 -v 25    # l:学习率 s:放缩比例 e:迭代次数 c:类别数 b:批量大小 v:验证集占比（除以100后为比率） 更多参数可以参考unet_torch项目中的markdown文档"><pre class="notranslate"><code>python train.py -l 0.0002 -s 0.5 -e 2 -c 3 -b 4 -v 25    # l:学习率 s:放缩比例 e:迭代次数 c:类别数 b:批量大小 v:验证集占比（除以100后为比率） 更多参数可以参考unet_torch项目中的markdown文档
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220823100017233.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220823100017233.png" alt="image-20220823100017233" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">输出“checkpoint xx saved！”即说明训练成功。在我们指定的checkpoint路径下可以找到训练好checkpoint模型参数文件</p>
<p dir="auto">3.简单测试一下已经训练好的模型的预测功能，在command中输入例如：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="python predict_custom.py -m checkpoint_new\checkpoint_epoch29.pth -i test\photo_19700101_000723.jpg -v -n
#-m:checkpoint文件路径  -i:需要预测的图片路径  -v:预测结果图片显示  -n:预测结果不再存储...
#更多参数可以参考该项目下的readme.md"><pre class="notranslate"><code>python predict_custom.py -m checkpoint_new\checkpoint_epoch29.pth -i test\photo_19700101_000723.jpg -v -n
#-m:checkpoint文件路径  -i:需要预测的图片路径  -v:预测结果图片显示  -n:预测结果不再存储...
#更多参数可以参考该项目下的readme.md
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">结果：</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220823115854084.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220823115854084.png" alt="image-20220823115854084" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="             从左到右，依次为：原图，road类（黄），grass类（黄），background类（黄）"><pre class="notranslate"><code>             从左到右，依次为：原图，road类（黄），grass类（黄），background类（黄）
</code></pre></div>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-5在算力服务平台训练模型" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#5在算力服务平台训练模型"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>5.在算力服务平台训练模型</h2>
<p dir="auto">1.本次实验我们在中科曙光的曙光智算平台训练我们的模型。在平台注册账号后，购买或者领取后，直接进入控制台。</p>
  <p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220823141415951.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220823141415951.png" alt="image-20220823141415951" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">2.配置环境</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220823141640985.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220823141640985.png" alt="image-20220823141640985" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">页面顶栏中命令行可以打开linux终端，E-File打开可视化文件管理</p>
  <p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220823145113434.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220823145113434.png" alt="image-20220823145113434" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">可视化编辑文件夹的功能非常方便，可以专门把接下来的安装包放入其中</p>
<p dir="auto">（1）安装anaconda：方法一：终端执行命令</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="wget https://repo.anaconda.com/archive/Anaconda3-2022.05-Linux-x86_64.sh     #直从官网下载安装包"><pre class="notranslate"><code>wget https://repo.anaconda.com/archive/Anaconda3-2022.05-Linux-x86_64.sh     #直从官网下载安装包
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">方法二：将.sh安装包下载到本地，再利用E-File 的上传功能把安装包上传到指定目录下。<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220823143111544.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220823143111544.png" alt="image-20220823143111544" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">（2）安装软件，并将anaconda添加到环境中</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="chmod +x ./Anaconda3-2022.05-Linux-x86_64.sh #随后运行"><pre class="notranslate"><code>chmod +x ./Anaconda3-2022.05-Linux-x86_64.sh #随后运行
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">安装完成后运行命令：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="source ~/.bashrc"><pre class="notranslate"><code>source ~/.bashrc
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">与在windows中同样的，安装完成后我们需要检查一次anaconda是否配置到了系统环境中。</p>
<p dir="auto">在终端中输入：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="conda"><pre class="notranslate"><code>conda
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">回车，若报错则需要手动将anaconda添加到环境中。</p>
<p dir="auto">添加方法如下：在终端中输入</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="nano ~/.bashrc"><pre class="notranslate"><code>nano ~/.bashrc
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">进入页面：</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220823154548326.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220823154548326.png" alt="image-20220823154548326" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">在其中的某个空白行上，填入anaconda的bin文件夹的路径：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="export PATH=/public/home/acddp272rz/anaconda3/bin:$PATH"><pre class="notranslate"><code>export PATH=/public/home/acddp272rz/anaconda3/bin:$PATH
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">添加的格式与路径上下对应如图：</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220823154712496.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220823154712496.png" alt="image-20220823154712496" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">添加完成后按 “ctrl+x”退出，选择确认保存即可。</p>
<p dir="auto">（3）配置虚拟环境</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="   ① 进入虚拟环境，值得注意的一点是，进入环境时可能会报错："><pre class="notranslate"><code>   ① 进入虚拟环境，值得注意的一点是，进入环境时可能会报错：
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220823162803122.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220823162803122.png" alt="image-20220823162803122" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">出现这种情况，运行：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="source activate  "><pre class="notranslate"><code>source activate  
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">再重新进入环境，即可解决问题。</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="②安装依赖的包，两种方法："><pre class="notranslate"><code>②安装依赖的包，两种方法：
</code></pre></div>

<p dir="auto">按照文档一步一步按照pytorch，以及其依赖包。安装完成后，再根据我们的训练项目py文件中所引用的包，以及运行后出现的“不存在xx包”的报错信息，用pip install命令，一步一步吧所需的包安装进环境里。</p>

</code></pre></div>

<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220823205012345.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220823205012345.png" alt="image-20220823205012345" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-6鸟瞰图变换" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#6鸟瞰图变换"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>6.鸟瞰图变换</h2>
<p dir="auto">1.相机成像原理与标定：对物理世界的任一点，推断它在照片上的位置，我们需要以下步骤：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=" ①世界坐标系→相机坐标系：由相机位置决定

 ② 相机坐标系→图像物理坐标系：按成像位置距离小孔之比，等比例放缩照片平面的x,y轴

 ③图像物理坐标系→图像像素坐标系 ：取图像某边角像素点为原点，根据像素点与物理长度之比和像素中心点位置的像素坐标，通过线性变换，计算得到某一点的像素点坐标"><pre class="notranslate"><code> ①世界坐标系→相机坐标系：由相机位置决定

 ② 相机坐标系→图像物理坐标系：按成像位置距离小孔之比，等比例放缩照片平面的x,y轴

 ③图像物理坐标系→图像像素坐标系 ：取图像某边角像素点为原点，根据像素点与物理长度之比和像素中心点位置的像素坐标，通过线性变换，计算得到某一点的像素点坐标
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">将以上数学计算全部整理为矩阵计算的形式，方便代码处理。</p>
<p dir="auto">视角位置影响来源于①（外参），畸变影响来源于②③（内参）。</p>
<p dir="auto">在训练完Unet网络后，我们可以对摄像头拍摄来的每一张照片做语义分割，分类出每一个属于道路的像素点，但仅有这个分类好的照片，我们仍不能精确的为我们的小车规划路径，因为我们的道路照片是扭曲且倾斜的，我们需要一个平面的鸟瞰图才能规划好小车的路径，而有了分类出道路的照片后，我们要做的，就是将上述过程反过来推演，通过照片上道路像素点的位置，找到道路像素点在真实物理世界中的位置（或者说在一个平面的类似地图的物理模型中的位置）。</p>
<p dir="auto">2.matlab成像实验：</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220824094537832.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220824094537832.png" alt="image-20220824094537832" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
  <p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220824094710714.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220824094710714.png" alt="image-20220824094710714" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="                 （上图为去畸变后，下图为去畸变前）"><pre class="notranslate"><code>                 （上图为去畸变后，下图为去畸变前）
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220824094745959.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220824094745959.png" alt="image-20220824094745959" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p> 
<p dir="auto">3.python成像实验</p>
<p dir="auto">（1）内参方面——表格去畸变案例，以及过程分析：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="①设置客观存在的物点

②对一张图片进行扫描，检测期盘格角点

③将物点与角点一一对应，完成去畸变（左为去畸变前，右为对棋盘去畸变后）："><pre class="notranslate"><code>①设置客观存在的物点

②对一张图片进行扫描，检测期盘格角点

③将物点与角点一一对应，完成去畸变（左为去畸变前，右为对棋盘去畸变后）：
</code></pre></div>
  <p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220824105231262.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220824105231262.png" alt="image-20220824105231262" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="④存储K D r t等值参数（畸变参数，旋转参数，平移参数）"><pre class="notranslate"><code>④存储K D r t等值参数（畸变参数，旋转参数，平移参数）
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">（2）外参方面——棋盘的鸟瞰图变换实验：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="  （作图为变换前，右图为鸟瞰变换后）&lt;img src=&quot;picture\image-20220824111352597.png&quot; alt=&quot;image-20220824111352597&quot; style=&quot;zoom:80%;&quot; /&gt;"><pre class="notranslate"><code>  （作图为变换前，右图为鸟瞰变换后）&lt;img src="picture\image-20220824111352597.png" alt="image-20220824111352597" style="zoom:80%;" /&gt;
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">原棋盘图片的四角点是由函数自行搜索得到，鸟瞰图变换后生成的棋盘的四角像素坐标位置可以自行指定。</p>
<p dir="auto">矫正完成后，得到矫正参数文件，在之后的小车中，因为我们的小车摄像头硬件，以及小车的摆放位置是固定的，直接调用我们的矫正参数就可以了.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-7路径规划与路径跟踪算法" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#7路径规划与路径跟踪算法"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>7.路径规划与路径跟踪算法</h2>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#PATH:\car_project\Astar
#PATH:\car_project\stanley"><pre class="notranslate"><code>#PATH:\car_project\Astar
#PATH:\car_project\stanley
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">1.在对像素已经打上标签的图片做鸟瞰图变换之后，我们就相当于得到了一张张“地图”，这些“地图”明确标好了那些是路，哪些地方不可以走。下一步，就是要根据这些“地图”，通过算法，计算出从出发点到终点的路径。</p>
<p dir="auto">（1）广度优先算法：</p>
<p dir="auto">从初始节点开始，先逐一探索初始节点的周边第一层节点，检查目标节点是否在这些节点中，若没有，再将所有第一层的节点逐一扩展，得到第二层节点，并逐一检查第二层节点中是否包含目标节点。若没有，再逐一扩展第二层的所有节点……，如此依次扩展，检查下去，直到发现目标节点为止。</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220824145015437.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220824145015437.png" alt="image-20220824145015437" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">（2）迪克斯特拉（Dijkstra）算法：</p>
<p dir="auto">从下一步可能要走的点中取出距离起点最小路径的点，走这个点，并以这个点为桥梁更新，求出下一个距离起点最小路径的点，直至到达终点，这样就找到了从起点到终点最近的那条路。</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220824144941891.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220824144941891.png" alt="image-20220824144941891" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">（3）贪心算法：</p>
<p dir="auto">只考虑，局部状态下，哪一步最能缩短自己位置与终点的距离，便执行哪一步，直到到达终点。</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220824150448895.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220824150448895.png" alt="image-20220824150448895" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">（4）A*算法：</p>
<p dir="auto">A*算法在上面那些算法的基础上，引入了启发式搜索，实际上是综合上面这些算法的特点于一身的。</p>
<p dir="auto">A*算法通过一个函数，对每一个节点做代价评估，区分每个节点的优先级：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="                                                    f(n)  =  g(n)  +  h(n)"><pre class="notranslate"><code>                                                    f(n)  =  g(n)  +  h(n)
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">其中：</p>
<p dir="auto">①f(n)是节点n的综合优先级。当我们选择下一个要遍历的节点时，我们总会选取综合优先级最高（值最小）的节点。</p>
<p dir="auto">②g(n) 是节点n距离起点的代价。</p>
<p dir="auto">③h(n)是节点n距离终点的预计代价，这也就是A*算法的启发函数。</p>
<p dir="auto">A*算法在运算过程中，每次从优先队列中选取f(n)值最小（优先级最高）的节点作为下一个待遍历的节点，另外可以发现，当启发函数h(n)  =  0 时，A *算法实际上变为了 Dijkstra’s Algorithm 算法。</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220824151902402.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220824151902402.png" alt="image-20220824151902402" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">2.python 的A*算法实验：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="PATH:\car_project\Astar   #该小项目的目录"><pre class="notranslate"><code>PATH:\car_project\Astar   #该小项目的目录
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220824154344047.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220824154344047.png" alt="image-20220824154344047" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">3.路径跟踪与Pure Pursuit算法：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="在我们的利用路径规划算法找到一条可行的道路后，我们就需要确保如何才能让小车按既定的路线去行驶。我们已经可以控制小车自由的直行，转弯，停止等，而要想根据路线精确控制小车运动，这就需要我们对小车及其运动建模并研究了。"><pre class="notranslate"><code>在我们的利用路径规划算法找到一条可行的道路后，我们就需要确保如何才能让小车按既定的路线去行驶。我们已经可以控制小车自由的直行，转弯，停止等，而要想根据路线精确控制小车运动，这就需要我们对小车及其运动建模并研究了。
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">（1）阿克曼转向几何模型：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="      理想的阿克曼转向，汽车在转弯的时候，两个轮胎的中轴指向同一个原点（如下），有了这个保证，我们可以进一步简化小车运动的模型为二维自行车模型。"><pre class="notranslate"><code>      理想的阿克曼转向，汽车在转弯的时候，两个轮胎的中轴指向同一个原点（如下），有了这个保证，我们可以进一步简化小车运动的模型为二维自行车模型。
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\v2-6df5463a76c7eaca5f04ccc461274c55_r.jpg"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\v2-6df5463a76c7eaca5f04ccc461274c55_r.jpg" alt="v2-6df5463a76c7eaca5f04ccc461274c55_r" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p> 
<p dir="auto">（2）二维自行车模型：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="    ①车辆只有前、后两个车轮；

    ②只考虑二维平面的运动，不考虑垂直方向的运功；

    ③车辆低速运动，此时滑移角可以忽略不计。"><pre class="notranslate"><code>    ①车辆只有前、后两个车轮；

    ②只考虑二维平面的运动，不考虑垂直方向的运功；

    ③车辆低速运动，此时滑移角可以忽略不计。
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">（3）基于上面的模型，我们可以通过下面的计算得到小车的转角关于时间，小车轴距，以及出发点到下一个目标点的函数：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="                                                &lt;img src=&quot;picture\image-20220824185728931.png&quot; alt=&quot;image-20220824185728931&quot; style=&quot;zoom: 50%;&quot; /&gt; 

                                 L：小车轴距            σ：小车某一时刻的转角         R：给定转角后，小车后路所遵循的圆的半径

                                                                       而我们目标即为求出σ，或者求出R（目前只有L已知）

                                             &lt;img src=&quot;picture\image-20220824190718821.png&quot; alt=&quot;image-20220824190718821&quot; style=&quot;zoom:50%;&quot; /&gt; "><pre class="notranslate"><code>                                                &lt;img src="picture\image-20220824185728931.png" alt="image-20220824185728931" style="zoom: 50%;" /&gt; 

                                 L：小车轴距            σ：小车某一时刻的转角         R：给定转角后，小车后路所遵循的圆的半径

                                                                       而我们目标即为求出σ，或者求出R（目前只有L已知）

                                             &lt;img src="picture\image-20220824190718821.png" alt="image-20220824190718821" style="zoom:50%;" /&gt; 
</code></pre></div>

</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">4.python Pure Pursuit模拟小车路径跟踪</p>

</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220824182122822.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220824182122822.png" alt="image-20220824182122822" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-8元器件测速计和imu" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#8元器件测速计和imu"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>8.元器件：测速计和IMU</h2>
<p dir="auto">1.测速计:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="本实验用到的是透光式测速传感器，主要由三个组成部分，分别是带孔的回盘、光源和光电管。圆盘随被测轴旋转时，光线只能通过因孔或缺口照射到光电管上。光电管被照射时，其反向电阻很低，于是输出一个电脉冲信号。光源被圆盘遮住时，光电管反向电阻很大，输出端就没有信号输出。这样，根据圆盘上的孔数或缺口数，即可测出被测轴的转速。

VCC——接5V电源          GND——接地             OUT——信号输出口，接在任意io脚，代码声明"><pre class="notranslate"><code>本实验用到的是透光式测速传感器，主要由三个组成部分，分别是带孔的回盘、光源和光电管。圆盘随被测轴旋转时，光线只能通过因孔或缺口照射到光电管上。光电管被照射时，其反向电阻很低，于是输出一个电脉冲信号。光源被圆盘遮住时，光电管反向电阻很大，输出端就没有信号输出。这样，根据圆盘上的孔数或缺口数，即可测出被测轴的转速。

VCC——接5V电源          GND——接地             OUT——信号输出口，接在任意io脚，代码声明
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">2.IMU:</p>
<p dir="auto">VCC——接3.3V电源        GND——接地            int——激活口，接在io脚即可         SDA——数据传输口，接主板SDA口       SCL——计时用，接小车主板SDA口</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220825143943365.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture\image-20220825143943365.png" alt="image-20220825143943365" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">上电后可以通过串口监听小车主板，输出的X,Y,Z为模块的位置初值，计算初值需要一定时间，此时不能移动小车或模块。</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="IMU可以测量车辆运动时的角速度和加速度，根据时间可以计算出小车的位移和运动角度，但计算位移时容易误差过大，故多用来计算小车角度(一次积分计算)。在工作时IMU模块容易受到周围强磁影响，需要放置于与其他模块有一定距离的地方，且工作时不可随意碰动，需要水平固定在小车上。"><pre class="notranslate"><code>IMU可以测量车辆运动时的角速度和加速度，根据时间可以计算出小车的位移和运动角度，但计算位移时容易误差过大，故多用来计算小车角度(一次积分计算)。在工作时IMU模块容易受到周围强磁影响，需要放置于与其他模块有一定距离的地方，且工作时不可随意碰动，需要水平固定在小车上。
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">3.调节实验</p>
<p dir="auto">（1）光电速度传感器直接读取的是舵机的转速，我们需要一个计算公式将转身转化为小车实际的行驶速度，这个公式写在小车主板的程序中，需要根据每个小车不同的安装情况自行计算。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-c notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#PATH:

if(millis() - old_millis &gt;= 500){
    car_speed = (count / 18.0 / 21 * 6.2 * 3.14 * 1000 / 500)* 0.75;
    count = 0;
    old_millis = millis();
  }"><pre>#PATH:

<span class="pl-k">if</span>(millis() - old_millis &gt;= <span class="pl-c1">500</span>){
    car_speed = (count / <span class="pl-c1">18.0</span> / <span class="pl-c1">21</span> * <span class="pl-c1">6.2</span> * <span class="pl-c1">3.14</span> * <span class="pl-c1">1000</span> / <span class="pl-c1">500</span>)* <span class="pl-c1">0.75</span>;
    count = <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
    old_millis = <span class="pl-c1">millis</span>();
  }</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">（2）可以用python发送请求获取小车的车速（如下）。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="import requests
import time

r = requests.get('http://192.168.4.1/read_speed')
print(r.text)
time.sleep(3)
r = requests.post('http://192.168.4.1/motor_control?speed=0')"><pre><span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">requests</span>

<p dir="auto">（3）启动小车电源后，reset主板，再待IMU模块重新矫正完毕，在小车不动的情况下，运行以上代码，获取小车转动角度值，以此来检验一下IMU工作是否稳定，若输出为一个接近0的值，说明IMU正常工作。再试试手动将小车转动90度，再次运行上述代码，若输出值接近90或者270度，说明IMU正常工作。</p>
