<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-9无人驾驶" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#9无人驾驶"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>9.无人驾驶</h2>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#PATH:\car_project\final"><pre class="notranslate"><code>#PATH:\car_project\final
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">以上的准备工作，一步一步规划好了我们无人驾驶的整个过程。而接下来我们可以通过简单分析无人驾驶的最终实现代码，更深入的了解整个过程。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#PATH:\car_project\final\final.py

import cv2
import numpy as np
from urllib.request import urlopen
import threading
import time
import torch
from PIL import Image
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

from pure_pursuit.utils import car_controllor, VehicleState, pure_pursuit_control
from seg import unet_predict
from seg.unet import UNet
from path_plan.utils import find_path

def read_ip_camera(stream):

    global url
    global img
    global bts
    global is_exit

    count = 0
    while not is_exit:
        try:
            bts += stream.read(CAMERA_BUFFRER_SIZE)
            jpghead=bts.find(b'\xff\xd8')
            jpgend=bts.find(b'\xff\xd9')
            
            if jpghead &gt; -1 and jpgend &gt; -1:
                print(count)
                count += 1
                jpg = bts[jpghead:jpgend + 2]
                bts = bts[jpgend + 2:]
                img = cv2.imdecode(np.frombuffer(jpg, dtype = np.uint8), cv2.IMREAD_UNCHANGED)

        except Exception as e:
            print(&quot;Error:&quot; + str(e))
            bts = b''
            stream = urlopen(url)
            continue

'''
主程序
'''
if __name__ == '__main__':
    #过程图像是否展示(有利于分析过程)
    SHOW_IMAGE = True
    #开头先看摄像头，因为我们小车自动行驶的第一步就是观察前方路况
    url = 'http://192.168.4.5:80/'
    stream = urlopen(url)
    CAMERA_BUFFRER_SIZE = 4096
    bts = b''
    img = None
    is_exit = False

    # 开始 imu 读取线程 保证摄像头读取与其他程序正常进行
    t1 = threading.Thread(target=read_ip_camera, args=(stream, ))
    t1.setDaemon(True)
    t1.start()

    time.sleep(5)
    
    #加载道路分割Unet模型，准备预测图片，模型参数为我们独立训练出的
    net = UNet(n_channels=3, n_classes=3, bilinear=False)
    device = torch.device('cuda' if torch.cuda.is_available() else 'cpu')
    net.to(device=device)
    net.load_state_dict(torch.load('seg\checkpoints\checkpoint_epoch1.pth', map_location=device))
    
    if SHOW_IMAGE:
        plt.imshow(img[:, :, [2,1,0]])
        plt.show()

    ctrller = car_controllor()
    
    #循环十次：拍照--处理图片--路径规划--决策--拍照.......
    for i in range(10):
        
        #Unet模型预测照片，给照片每一个像素点打标签
        img_Image = Image.fromarray(img)
        mask = unet_predict.predict_img(net=net,
                            full_img=img_Image,
                            scale_factor=0.5,
                            out_threshold=0.5,
                            device=device)
        mask = unet_predict.mask_to_image(mask)
        
        if SHOW_IMAGE:
            plt.imshow(mask)
            plt.show()
       
        #决策寻路，其中find_path为关键函数，集合了去畸变，鸟瞰变换，图片进一步优化，路径规划于一身
        #用一个try的结构去判断：如果前面没有可行驶的路，那么后退四秒
        try:
            path = find_path(mask, time_limit=5, SHOW_IMAGE=SHOW_IMAGE)
        except:
            ctrller.motor_control(-50)
            time.sleep(4)
            ctrller.motor_control(0)
            continue

        path_array = np.array(path)
        path_array = np.vstack((path_array[:, 1], path_array[:, 0])).T
        path_array[:, 1] = 29 - path_array[:, 1]
        path_array = path_array * 40
        print(path_array)  #输出路径

        if SHOW_IMAGE:
            plt.figure()
            plt.scatter(path_array[:, 0], path_array[:, 1], s=20, c='red', alpha=0.6)
            plt.show()


        '''
        路线跟踪常量
        '''
        Lf = 100.0  # look-ahead distance 前视觉距离
        dt = 1.0  # [s]  
        d = 144.0  # [mm] wheel base of vehicle 车轴长度
        delta_candicate = np.array([-28, -16.2, 0.0, 16.2, 28]) / 180 * np.pi
        delta_cmd = np.array([90, 60, 0, -60, -90], np.int16) + 90

        ctrller.servo_control(90)
        ctrller.motor_control(50)
        state = VehicleState(x=800, y=0, delta=0.0, yaw=0, v=0)

        # 1 px = 40 mm 控制小车按规划的路径行驶
        pure_pursuit_control(state, path_array, ctrller)

    is_exit = True
    t1.join()"><pre><span class="pl-c">#PATH:\car_project\final\final.py</span>

<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">cv2</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">numpy</span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s1">np</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">urllib</span>.<span class="pl-s1">request</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">urlopen</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">threading</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">time</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">torch</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-v">PIL</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">Image</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">matplotlib</span>.<span class="pl-s1">pyplot</span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s1">plt</span>

<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">pure_pursuit</span>.<span class="pl-s1">utils</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">car_controllor</span>, <span class="pl-v">VehicleState</span>, <span class="pl-s1">pure_pursuit_control</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">seg</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">unet_predict</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">seg</span>.<span class="pl-s1">unet</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">UNet</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">path_plan</span>.<span class="pl-s1">utils</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">find_path</span>

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">read_ip_camera</span>(<span class="pl-s1">stream</span>):

    <span class="pl-k">global</span> <span class="pl-s1">url</span>
    <span class="pl-k">global</span> <span class="pl-s1">img</span>
    <span class="pl-k">global</span> <span class="pl-s1">bts</span>
    <span class="pl-k">global</span> <span class="pl-s1">is_exit</span>

    <span class="pl-s1">count</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>
    <span class="pl-k">while</span> <span class="pl-c1">not</span> <span class="pl-s1">is_exit</span>:
        <span class="pl-k">try</span>:
            <span class="pl-s1">bts</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s1">stream</span>.<span class="pl-en">read</span>(<span class="pl-v">CAMERA_BUFFRER_SIZE</span>)
            <span class="pl-s1">jpghead</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">bts</span>.<span class="pl-en">find</span>(<span class="pl-s">b'<span class="pl-cce">\xff</span><span class="pl-cce">\xd8</span>'</span>)
            <span class="pl-s1">jpgend</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">bts</span>.<span class="pl-en">find</span>(<span class="pl-s">b'<span class="pl-cce">\xff</span><span class="pl-cce">\xd9</span>'</span>)
            
            <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">jpghead</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span> <span class="pl-c1">and</span> <span class="pl-s1">jpgend</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span>:
                <span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s1">count</span>)
                <span class="pl-s1">count</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>
                <span class="pl-s1">jpg</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">bts</span>[<span class="pl-s1">jpghead</span>:<span class="pl-s1">jpgend</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>]
                <span class="pl-s1">bts</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">bts</span>[<span class="pl-s1">jpgend</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>:]
                <span class="pl-s1">img</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">cv2</span>.<span class="pl-en">imdecode</span>(<span class="pl-s1">np</span>.<span class="pl-en">frombuffer</span>(<span class="pl-s1">jpg</span>, <span class="pl-s1">dtype</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">np</span>.<span class="pl-s1">uint8</span>), <span class="pl-s1">cv2</span>.<span class="pl-v">IMREAD_UNCHANGED</span>)

        <span class="pl-k">except</span> <span class="pl-v">Exception</span> <span class="pl-k">as</span> <span class="pl-s1">e</span>:
            <span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"Error:"</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-en">str</span>(<span class="pl-s1">e</span>))
            <span class="pl-s1">bts</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">b''</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">stream</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">urlopen</span>(<span class="pl-s1">url</span>)
            <span class="pl-k">continue</span>

<span class="pl-s">'''</span>
<span class="pl-s">主程序</span>
<span class="pl-s">'''</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">__name__</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">'__main__'</span>:
    <span class="pl-c">#过程图像是否展示(有利于分析过程)</span>
    <span class="pl-v">SHOW_IMAGE</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">True</span>
    <span class="pl-c">#开头先看摄像头，因为我们小车自动行驶的第一步就是观察前方路况</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">url</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">'http://192.168.4.5:80/'</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">stream</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">urlopen</span>(<span class="pl-s1">url</span>)
    <span class="pl-v">CAMERA_BUFFRER_SIZE</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">4096</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">bts</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">b''</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">img</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">None</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">is_exit</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">False</span>

    <span class="pl-c"># 开始 imu 读取线程 保证摄像头读取与其他程序正常进行</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">t1</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">threading</span>.<span class="pl-v">Thread</span>(<span class="pl-s1">target</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">read_ip_camera</span>, <span class="pl-s1">args</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span>(<span class="pl-s1">stream</span>, ))
    <span class="pl-s1">t1</span>.<span class="pl-en">setDaemon</span>(<span class="pl-c1">True</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">t1</span>.<span class="pl-en">start</span>()

    <span class="pl-s1">time</span>.<span class="pl-en">sleep</span>(<span class="pl-c1">5</span>)
    
    <span class="pl-c">#加载道路分割Unet模型，准备预测图片，模型参数为我们独立训练出的</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">net</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">UNet</span>(<span class="pl-s1">n_channels</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">3</span>, <span class="pl-s1">n_classes</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">3</span>, <span class="pl-s1">bilinear</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">False</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">device</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">torch</span>.<span class="pl-en">device</span>(<span class="pl-s">'cuda'</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">torch</span>.<span class="pl-s1">cuda</span>.<span class="pl-en">is_available</span>() <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-s">'cpu'</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">net</span>.<span class="pl-en">to</span>(<span class="pl-s1">device</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">device</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">net</span>.<span class="pl-en">load_state_dict</span>(<span class="pl-s1">torch</span>.<span class="pl-en">load</span>(<span class="pl-s">'seg\checkpoints\checkpoint_epoch1.pth'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">map_location</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">device</span>))
    
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-v">SHOW_IMAGE</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">plt</span>.<span class="pl-en">imshow</span>(<span class="pl-s1">img</span>[:, :, [<span class="pl-c1">2</span>,<span class="pl-c1">1</span>,<span class="pl-c1">0</span>]])
        <span class="pl-s1">plt</span>.<span class="pl-en">show</span>()

    <span class="pl-s1">ctrller</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">car_controllor</span>()
    
    <span class="pl-c">#循环十次：拍照--处理图片--路径规划--决策--拍照.......</span>
    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">range</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>):
        
        <span class="pl-c">#Unet模型预测照片，给照片每一个像素点打标签</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">img_Image</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">Image</span>.<span class="pl-en">fromarray</span>(<span class="pl-s1">img</span>)
        <span class="pl-s1">mask</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">unet_predict</span>.<span class="pl-en">predict_img</span>(<span class="pl-s1">net</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">net</span>,
                            <span class="pl-s1">full_img</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">img_Image</span>,
                            <span class="pl-s1">scale_factor</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">0.5</span>,
                            <span class="pl-s1">out_threshold</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">0.5</span>,
                            <span class="pl-s1">device</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">device</span>)
        <span class="pl-s1">mask</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">unet_predict</span>.<span class="pl-en">mask_to_image</span>(<span class="pl-s1">mask</span>)
        
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-v">SHOW_IMAGE</span>:
            <span class="pl-s1">plt</span>.<span class="pl-en">imshow</span>(<span class="pl-s1">mask</span>)
            <span class="pl-s1">plt</span>.<span class="pl-en">show</span>()
       
        <span class="pl-c">#决策寻路，其中find_path为关键函数，集合了去畸变，鸟瞰变换，图片进一步优化，路径规划于一身</span>
        <span class="pl-c">#用一个try的结构去判断：如果前面没有可行驶的路，那么后退四秒</span>
        <span class="pl-k">try</span>:
            <span class="pl-s1">path</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">find_path</span>(<span class="pl-s1">mask</span>, <span class="pl-s1">time_limit</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">5</span>, <span class="pl-v">SHOW_IMAGE</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-v">SHOW_IMAGE</span>)
        <span class="pl-k">except</span>:
            <span class="pl-s1">ctrller</span>.<span class="pl-en">motor_control</span>(<span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">50</span>)
            <span class="pl-s1">time</span>.<span class="pl-en">sleep</span>(<span class="pl-c1">4</span>)
            <span class="pl-s1">ctrller</span>.<span class="pl-en">motor_control</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>)
            <span class="pl-k">continue</span>

        <span class="pl-s1">path_array</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">np</span>.<span class="pl-en">array</span>(<span class="pl-s1">path</span>)
        <span class="pl-s1">path_array</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">np</span>.<span class="pl-en">vstack</span>((<span class="pl-s1">path_array</span>[:, <span class="pl-c1">1</span>], <span class="pl-s1">path_array</span>[:, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>])).<span class="pl-v">T</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">path_array</span>[:, <span class="pl-c1">1</span>] <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">29</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">path_array</span>[:, <span class="pl-c1">1</span>]
        <span class="pl-s1">path_array</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">path_array</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-c1">40</span>
        <span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s1">path_array</span>)  <span class="pl-c">#输出路径</span>

        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-v">SHOW_IMAGE</span>:
            <span class="pl-s1">plt</span>.<span class="pl-en">figure</span>()
            <span class="pl-s1">plt</span>.<span class="pl-en">scatter</span>(<span class="pl-s1">path_array</span>[:, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>], <span class="pl-s1">path_array</span>[:, <span class="pl-c1">1</span>], <span class="pl-s1">s</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">20</span>, <span class="pl-s1">c</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'red'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">alpha</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">0.6</span>)
            <span class="pl-s1">plt</span>.<span class="pl-en">show</span>()


        <span class="pl-s">'''</span>
<span class="pl-s">        路线跟踪常量</span>
<span class="pl-s">        '''</span>
        <span class="pl-v">Lf</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">100.0</span>  <span class="pl-c"># look-ahead distance 前视觉距离</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">dt</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">1.0</span>  <span class="pl-c"># [s]  </span>
        <span class="pl-s1">d</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">144.0</span>  <span class="pl-c"># [mm] wheel base of vehicle 车轴长度</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">delta_candicate</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">np</span>.<span class="pl-en">array</span>([<span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">28</span>, <span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">16.2</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0.0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">16.2</span>, <span class="pl-c1">28</span>]) <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">180</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">np</span>.<span class="pl-s1">pi</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">delta_cmd</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">np</span>.<span class="pl-en">array</span>([<span class="pl-c1">90</span>, <span class="pl-c1">60</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">60</span>, <span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-c1">90</span>], <span class="pl-s1">np</span>.<span class="pl-s1">int16</span>) <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">90</span>

        <span class="pl-s1">ctrller</span>.<span class="pl-en">servo_control</span>(<span class="pl-c1">90</span>)
        <span class="pl-s1">ctrller</span>.<span class="pl-en">motor_control</span>(<span class="pl-c1">50</span>)
        <span class="pl-s1">state</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-v">VehicleState</span>(<span class="pl-s1">x</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">800</span>, <span class="pl-s1">y</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-s1">delta</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">0.0</span>, <span class="pl-s1">yaw</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-s1">v</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">0</span>)

        <span class="pl-c"># 1 px = 40 mm 控制小车按规划的路径行驶</span>
        <span class="pl-en">pure_pursuit_control</span>(<span class="pl-s1">state</span>, <span class="pl-s1">path_array</span>, <span class="pl-s1">ctrller</span>)

    <span class="pl-s1">is_exit</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">True</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">t1</span>.<span class="pl-en">join</span>()</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">以下为某次无人驾驶实验从头到尾产出的过程，以及简单分析。</p>
<p dir="auto">道路照片</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162041408.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162041408.png" alt="image-20220826162041408" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Unet语义分割后</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162101313.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162101313.png" alt="image-20220826162101313" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">去畸变后</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162141820.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162141820.png" alt="image-20220826162141820" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">鸟瞰变换后</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162212007.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162212007.png" alt="image-20220826162212007" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">grass标签获取，并去除grass的小块区域</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162232819.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162232819.png" alt="image-20220826162232819" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">background标签，并除去background的小块区域</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162252131.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162252131.png" alt="image-20220826162252131" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">可视化，此时有四类像素，road，grass，background以及空白（鸟瞰变换形成或因属于游离的小区域而被删去）</p>
<p dir="auto">然后分别对grass和background做扩展，把边缘变得光滑</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162305495.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162305495.png" alt="image-20220826162305495" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">像素点缩放，缩放为每个像素点四厘米</p>
<p dir="auto">同时补全“空白”区域</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162320473.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162320473.png" alt="image-20220826162320473" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">去掉与起点无法连接的路</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162336952.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162336952.png" alt="image-20220826162336952" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162354119.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162354119.png" alt="image-20220826162354119" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">选取终点的弧：80cm</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162408261.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162408261.png" alt="image-20220826162408261" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">取到的可作为终点的点</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/blob/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162424983.png"><img src="/ZhaXionghui/automatic-mini-car/raw/main/smart_car/picture%5Cimage-20220826162424983.png" alt="image-20220826162424983" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">之后就是小车根据路径规划算法，找到对应路线，并通过路径跟踪，沿路线行驶至目标点。</p>
<p dir="auto">至此，本次无人驾驶项目至此完成。</p>
</article>
  </div>

    </div>

  </readme-toc>
